Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	When it is a certain way, you make three or four cauteries, along the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the fire in the liver that we have mentioned before; and do not press your hand on the entire cautery, and let the hairs be on its back; and another way of cauterizing is that you heat the cauterizer with two needles, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder; and lift the wound that is located near the mouse's ear, or the pain from the ear comes towards the left, and let the elevations that you lift the wound according to the curve, according to the length of the body, and the cauterizer should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After applying the two fingers and inflame them until the curved part is perceived from the other side, then draw out the cautery, and thus enter with four fingers. If you see, then cauterize the entire cautery with three fingers.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After treatment when the patient has gout due to long standing, and this is also useful for the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	of hydrops
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not useful for hydrops, except in the manner which is called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods that we have mentioned in the divisions, and your treatment does not help, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations around the belly, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one below the mouse, and one behind the back above the spine, and one in the worst place; and let the cauterizations be close to the curved part.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leaving the fire cautery open for a long time, do not neglect the care of the wound after the cauterization; and healing would hasten, and together with God's help, both intentions would be achieved.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the fire cauterization for the belly is like the one we have shown before; and for the back, it should be olive-shaped, according to what has been written before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet are swollen and have plain yellow wounds, it is necessary to cauterize above the back of the foot between the auricular and annular parts; and gently move your hand with the cauterization towards returning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, thus avoiding the yellowish part, and let the cauteries be done in this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After making two cuts on each leg at the tip of a sharp knife; and let the cauteries be long, one behind the knee in front and the other in front of the knee, inside the leg; and leave the cauteries hanging for a long time to cure the wound that is inside. After curing the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the solution of the belly comes from cold and moisture, as long as the retentive and digestive powers that are in the stomach and in the intestines are blocked, and cannot be cured by other means of treatment; and you see the pain is very severe and of great benefit, if you make a large cauterization on the stomach according to what it has spoken about before or a cauterization of the stomach, let the cauterization circulate; and four cauterizations around the belly subtly to all the sharp cauterization, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	If you see abundant moisture and the patient is suffering from pain, then perform fire cauterization on the joint, and I cauterize each wound, and II small cauterizations over the stomach below the large one, for the cure is beneficial when it has good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of lice
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the lice are firmly attached, or one or more, and are ancient and are large humors that are cold and moist and corrupted, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and it does not improve, then perform cauterizations: III over the spine of the back, which is all before unmedicated little by little in triangulating, and I cauterize outside the belly II doses; and if you think that his stomach is cooled, and the food does not cook, and one sees the face swells, then the face has I large cauterization over the stomach, as it is previously said, and I other over the liver, and I other over the mouse all the cauterization clavile; and leave the cauterization open long.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After care, the limb when it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the charnel pit which is called "thelul".
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you approach the charnel pit, if the caustic seems like a razor, and then put it all burned on top of the charnel pit covered; and let your hand so that the cauterizer comes to the birth of the vein, from which the blood flows; do this once or twice, and if there is much charnel pit, cauterize each one as we have said; then cure wounds as long as they are healed; and if you cauterize with a large caustic above the charnel pit, it will have more help.
de plaie mal curee	of poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the wound cannot bear a lancer or an opening, which we will tell you about in its place, then comes the disease that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any comes fistula, and is alert and poured with pus and corrupted moisture, then you must apply a thin tent throughout, and guard that you remove the entire tent as soon as it becomes full.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cauterizer, which seems like a razor, and pressing it into the fistula according to the amount that the tent has entered, and then reapplying the cauterizer until the corroding and corrupting parts are destroyed, once, or twice, or three times, depending on the amount of need; and guard against burning the nerves which are near, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the center of the bladder and intestine, you should avoid these areas, and only do so in cases where it is necessary, and think that it is not healed; after curing the area as long as it is healthy, and if the areas are sealed, and the matter is removed along with tension, then wash the areas that the area is completely healed; and if the matter is not removed, seal the area and corrupt the bone at the source; and thus as one of these that we will say in its area.
de la maladie des reins	of the kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When severe pain comes to the kidneys, and great swelling, and does not take on the form of a woman, then it is necessary that you apply cauterization to the kidneys on both sides with the clavile cautery that we have previously mentioned; and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in a line, and they will be greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is small and weak from heat and moisture, and it retains urine, then perform cauterization in the part before the bladder, where the hairs of the pubic area begin, on both sides, and each cautery should be as long as a pin; and perform one cauterization behind the back, or two if you have need; and let the cauteries be clavile according to the form previously mentioned.
de la marris	of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit. de la hainche	of the waist
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the thick viscous fluids descend to the hip of the waist, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and the legs are found to be uneven, it is necessary that you cauterize the pain above the hip of the waist with a cautery similar to a circle, and sign before the bone around the hip as it turns, so that the hip is inside the circle; and if it is such a cauterization as has been done for the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez. de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the back of the waist, and it is from cold and moisture, and the ailment is caused by what we have said in the division and the cure does not work, and the disease is ancient: therefore it is necessary that you purge the ailment of large humors with fetid pills, or other good-quality pills similar.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the firing; and the manner of the firing is as follows: that is to say together with burning medicines, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cauterization is in many ways, of which some are: that you cauterize above the back of the waist three triangular cauterizations according to this form, and make good depth and great, and there should be between each cauterization a space the size of a finger, and let the cauterization be olive; never made on the middle above the back of the waist, because it is there four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see that the cauterization is done with a circle as we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the shoulder; but do it in another manner so that the circle contains the entire shoulder and all the tendons should be arched.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in lithotomy, when the pain remains in the shoulder and does not reach the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it comes to the thigh and the leg, then make two cauterizations where the hairs are located, and one cauterization above the ankle four fingers wide, on the right side a little; and both cauterizations should be sharp, and the tendons should be arched; and if the hairs feel that the pain extends to the feet or near the knee, then cauterize where it feels the pain three points or four at the cauterization called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the profession is, do more to him; and if the pain is dislocated from the groin towards the thigh, apply cauterization with a surgical or circular cautery, and be careful in all your cauterizations that you do not leave the cautery for too long, burning nerves and large arteries, and do not cause greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I have also seen many who applied cauterization above the ankle, and left it for so long that the leg was entirely blackened, and the foot also, and all the flesh was rotten.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a purging of the stomach where they experienced death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in both parts together, perform cauterization in one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the wise say in the cauterization of the belly, of which this is the method, use such a sharp and as big as a navillon of a finger, or a little less, and it should be inserted between the ribs and inserted from one to the other at a distance equal to the amount of a small nail; and the ribs should be over two parts, and they should also be like a needle, and there is a good belly knife.
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And heat it until it is completely red and glowing, then place it on the back of the misaligned shoulder, and turn it over to the healthy side; and cauterize once with the cautery and leave it for three days; then apply a butter poultice, and keep the wound open for a long time; after the treatment of ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasis says that we use this cautery little because of its fearful appearance, and few see those who use it; and nevertheless, this is a good cauterizer, which can bear the pain, and where it is applied.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The fire cauteries are made such that you make an instrument of thin sheets of metal or iron at the edge of the door, and on one side, it is long, and on the other, it has two points, and on each side, there is the quantity of a small drop; and they are open below and above, and join together in this form:

After placing the bandage of the back hanging on its side, and quickly bringing your hand over the bandage of the back; afterwards, pour between the two circles of hot water that has been heated in the fire for a short time, and leave it an hour, and let the hairs suffer the heat and burn.

Because it is true that there are also cauterizations as of fire; and when the cauterizations have passed, gently remove your hand with the instrument and lift the backbone slightly, and leave it for three hours, and put butter on until the black scab of the burn is removed; and let it rest for three hours so that the wound may be healed; and this would be the last aid after the care of ointments as long as it is healthy.

And if the pain has extended to the thigh or to the leg, then make the instrument that tingles the back according to what you have done in the backbone; and this is the way of the hot needle, and I have written about it in the treatment of medicine correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take equal amounts of lime and live chalk, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	If there is a small hole where the point of a razor cannot fill it; and put that pot in another well-pounded pot, and put over it lime and chalk and pour warm water on it until there are two layers of powder, you will have it well prepared in your hand; and let it soak until all the water and chalk and lime have settled at the bottom, then take all the powder, and pour it through a sieve over lime and lime, as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble. Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galen tells us of a cure that some people were cured of the pain in the back and sciatic veins, and they were very much healed, and said that no other cure was done, and that they were cured once when this cure was made, and he was bathed as he teaches afterwards.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure. Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And let it be known that no one should use such cauteries or medicines unless after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides says that when the vein of the temple is cauterized with the fleece of a goat, it helps much; and it should be done by the cauterizer in this way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the other and the old oil, and put it on the groove that is between the thumb of one foot and the other which is called the first metacarpal.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	Then take some goat hair, and put it in the fire until it is charred, and put it on the cloth, and leave it until it is soaked; and do again in this way, and do not stop doing in this way until you think that it is close to the back, and that the pain has stopped; and this method of cauterization is called "goat hair cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	of great pain in two places
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or from impact or from too great evacuation, or from similar expanded cold matter, none of these things is worth cauterization, because it causes cold to those who have recently undergone infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary to apply foul-smelling powders or similar things, which are placed on top of the back, where the pain is located, three lines wide, and in each line five cauteries or more according to the strength and quantity that the pain can bear; and let the cauteries be made with the cautery called "puncture"; and if you see, make three or four cauteries with the middle-sized clavicle according to this form:

Often this disease comes to small children, and the signs of onset are that they have a stiff neck when walking, and fear; and you will see it in the last spinous process of the back and in us the appearance that comes above the other spinous processes.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you want to cure it, if you cauterize with the fire cautery in this form.

After healing the patient for as long as they are healthy according to what we have said, and ensure that you do not administer cauterization in a way that is painful or causes damage to the nerves.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the pain of the joints is due to moisture that is spread to each member of the body, and when the pain comes suddenly, which is properly called "gout", and when it is caused by cold and cannot be cured by medicines, then it must be treated with cauterization in this manner: apply a large amount of cauterizing agents around the joint, and let the cauterizing oils be applied in this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a belief that you should hold the face down during the cauterization, then perform the entire cauterization as claimed "not to point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come from the gums and other joints, and this often happens, then perform cauterization on each tooth with three or four cautery of each part, at the entire cauterization; and if you have more skill, do more, but do not hold your hand further than the end of the tooth until the spirit of the patient is calm.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the gums and back, then administer the cauterization that we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are severe, make a point around the nail II lines; and if it does not remain painful, make a point above each joint and above the hair of the hand; and if the pains come just at the wrist or shoulder, cauterize each part, and good governance to the patient and many medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good governance and purge the humor, it will be healed by the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the wound of the eye
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the wound comes in anger, and the pus descends to the joints and it is new, then you must wait until when you cure the eye, that he does not move much that day; and that he uses things that relieve the stomach, so that the feeling of the gut does not come out of his stomach; afterwards make him sit upright on his back between your hands, and command him to cover his eye as long as the pus is not restored, and roll it to your side, and sign over the wound above the bone of the thumb, and at all a sign that is similar to half a circle above the body; then heat the cautery with this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it is white and sweats senselessly.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the mud from the joint; and the ministers stain their hands above so they do not return back; and work well the thighs against the pain, and put disinfectant on him the castor and the serum above the thighs, and the other above the worst that stains his hands; then put the cautery on all of his hand, and hold it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, start again with another until you come just to the bone; and be careful that the mud does not come out when you do the cautery; that you do not burn it; and that by this the pain does not kill him, or other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And if you do not see the bone at the cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And the cauterization of children should be subtle according to their measure of bones, and for large people also large according to their measure; after three days care for the wound of the cautery with bread until the eschar is formed; then care for other inflammations as long as it is healthy, and cut the hairs 40 times on its back until the wound is well healed; and it should be that their movements are restricted for a long time, so that the pus does not seep out when they move around.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty days, when he wishes to get up, one should apply a well-made bandage for forty more days; and have good rest, that he works little and avoids too much drinking and eating, and too much high heat; and if he follows this instruction, he is completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will tell you about the treatment of cutting into his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not increase, one should apply the fire cautery according to its quantity, and let the third part of the care; after the cure as we have said; and none of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with the fire cautery at three angles in this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is to straighten the limb and make a line across the width of the fracture, and another one in front, and then apply your hand to all the cauterizing iron.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and less painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of ancient pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, whether it is to fall or to be injured, and this pain lasts long, and the medical cure does not help, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called «poins», and the cauterization should be according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and its virtue and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If it is safe for the first cautery, it is good; if not, begin another cautery above that one, for it is usually customary to let the patient die at the member where the injury is closest, because it is necessary to perform the cauterizations until the wounds are healed.
de meselerie	mesenteric
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The mesenteries are never cauterized by cauterization alone, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of fluids and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	If you see that the cauterization is not curing the disease at the beginning, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the previous section, and if it does not remain or disappear, and if you doubt that the corruption will not spread throughout the wound, then perform the following cauterizations: I on the forehead, and the other on the front of the head at the end of the eyebrows; II on the two temples, and I behind the ears; and leave as much space as possible between the cauterizations and the bone, and until the scabs come out so that the vapors of the large humors can escape; and then cauterize again according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And if the splinters are scattered throughout; and they are clearly visible, it is necessary that you cauterize with these cautery that we have said or chief, and the cautery in the nose, and two cauteries above the spine of the neck, and six cauteries above the spine of the back, and one great one above and one below the buttocks, and two above each shoulder, and two above the elbows, and two above the knees, and one above each hand and foot, and above the hand wounds; and beware of the nerves that are above the bones, that you do not burn them; and never make a cautery above the bone of the little finger, and one above the bone of the stomach, and one above the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And the more you use the cautery, the less you need assistance, and it benefits him; and the hairs do not feel pain as they do for the healthy one, because the body is already corrupt.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the cautery be large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in the manner of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the wound with flour and honey and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When inflammation comes to any member and is treated with medicines and oils and poultices, and it is not healed, then you should cauterize the member according to its size and smallness; and the cautery should go a little into the depth of the wound; then treat the boils until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And never cauterize with the hand and at the foot and at the back, after the nerve that moves the limb, and thus it is set in the swelling; and it does not interfere with anyone if they are not knowledgeable about the members and their issues of moving the body.
de albaras	And never cauterize with the hand and at
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the disease called «albaras» is awakened, and medical knowledge does not help, then cauterize with a cautery a little in front, according to the quantity of the herb, until the bones are set and the color is restored; then treat with flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and salt of colon and salt of almond, each in equal parts; and mix everything together, and bind it all with a cloth, and apply to the wound until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of chancres by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancres appears at the beginning, and you see it stop growing, then cauterize it with the cauterizing iron that seems to be in the shape of a circle, all around the edge of the chancres.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And all the wise say that one should also make the cauterizing iron in the middle of the chancres; and I do not think this is good, because I believe it should not be ulcerated or corrupted, and I have never seen it happen once; and a more important thing is that it should be cauterized all around, with the cauterizing iron that is called «circle», as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When anyone has a disease called "adubelati", and it lingers to die or due to the excess it causes or due to the age of the patient when they are too old and have little blood, or due to tension; then you see it hastening to die: therefore cauterize around with many small cauteries pricking; after leaving it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will surely die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through all the cauteries, then heat the cauteries with what is in its form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease that is called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced the skin, and be such cauteries that the hairs feel afterwards in a similar manner as the course of the porridge is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The cure of fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than a piece of member, for it twists the members as if the dry reeds did.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the limb that can suffer cauterization together with fire, then heat the cauteries cleverly very small and great, according to what is necessary for the limb or the disease; after cauterizing all parts until you reach all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that all that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days, and put oil on the wounds, cauterize with suffering until the scorched flesh is removed, and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of boils, ulcers arise.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that healthy ulcers do not arise, it is good; and if not, if the cauterization begins again on the part that remains corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this method has never been cured by medical plasters in place of fire cauterization; but fire cauterization is always greater help, and I have already told the cure of the medical plaster in the division: take it when you have occasion.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the pores that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	often comes to the feet through the pores, which is called "clos" according to our understanding, and is a great thing that causes pain in the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries of this disease are according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cauterization, and water hot cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is that you heat the cauterizer as if it were a quill, and it should be made of good iron at the measure that it can pierce the nail from all parts, and that it has thin margins; then put it all hot on the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches the end of the nail; and leave it thus for three days until it begins to rot; then make an ointment of wild savage herbs pounded with silk, and leave the ointment all night, and the nail will fall off and will be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cure the limb of burning by applying a cool herb until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted by previous burns, and often in hands and feet, then it is necessary to apply cauterization with very hot iron; and it is in this way: take a needle of iron or steel, or a pen of owl feathers, and place it on the nail and the cuticle, that is to say, the rough skin; then place the hot water on the needle so that it surrounds everything, then hold your hand tightly and press your hand as you turn so that the edge of the needle comes to the root of the nail, and find the very hot water penetrating deep into the root; and suffer the pain of the hot water for an hour; then leave it like this, and it will fall out at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Then do another one after that, until you have treated all those that are at the core, then treat the wounds that engender char.
li cure dou trembler	the treatment of the shaking
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When anyone shakes from cold or from a quartan fever or other, it is necessary to make four cauteries or four on the spine of the back; one cautery between each spine; and one cautery at the chest, and one above the stomach at the olive cauterization; it will let them shake, and hasten the recovery from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pustules that stink
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No matter how often the body is washed, or pustules appear, which come from large corrupt matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary when they appear that a cauterization be made over each head of the pustule: a subtle cauterizer of willow bark, of which the point is grasped in the fire, or of the long root of aristolochia, or with the lenticular cauterizer.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And no matter how often they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear, in this manner, and it cannot grow more, but is broken down the excess from which they come, and are healed; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times there is great bleeding from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes to the periphery, or at the incision of the abscess, or in the cauterization of the limb, and similar things; and it is a very painful thing to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And in any case when this happens to anyone, quickly place your finger on the wound of the vein, and press very hard until the bleeding is stopped from your finger, and no more blood comes out; then put the cauteries made of olive oil into the fire several times, both small and large, until they are all red; then apply I, or a great or little one according to the wound and the limb where the artery has been cut, and hold the cauteries on that vein where you placed your finger, and hold the cauteries there until the bleeding is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	If you suddenly fall forward while holding the other end of the cautery over the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, then quickly take another one that is at the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not cease to do this one after the other until the blood is stopped; and be careful that you do not burn the nerve that is next to it, and that no other misfortune comes over the wound; and see that when the artery is not cut off, it cannot be extinguished immediately when the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods we have mentioned: or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by a very thin thread, or by medicines placed above which have power to stop blood; and it should be tied and held tightly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever will administer the tightening of lacing or tying things together tightly over, or other similar things, does not benefit if not properly.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have any medicine present, they should put their two fingers on the wound of the vein as we have said, and well tighten until it is stopped up over the wound and over the vein; and they should not move it, but keep it cold with often cool water until it is frozen and swollen and stopped up; and they should make inquiries about what they have to do with cauteries and medicines.
